    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [c0].[Id], [c0].[BannerButtonText], [c0].[BannerText], [c0].[ButtonLink], [c0].[ButtonText], [c0].[ContentData], [c0].[ContentOrderNo], [c0].[ContentPageId], [c0].[ContentShort], [c0].[ContentTypesId], [c0].[CreaDate], [c0].[CreaUser], [c0].[Description], [c0].[ExternalLink], [c0].[FormTypeId], [c0].[IsActive], [c0].[IsBayi], [c0].[IsBireysel], [c0].[IsClick], [c0].[IsDeleted], [c0].[IsEndustri], [c0].[IsFooterMenu], [c0].[IsGallery], [c0].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c0].[IsHeaderMenu], [c0].[IsInteral], [c0].[IsInterax], [c0].[IsIntersecure], [c0].[IsInterwall], [c0].[IsMap], [c0].[IsMimar], [c0].[IsPublish], [c0].[IsSideMenu], [c0].[IsStatus], [c0].[LangId], [c0].[Link], [c0].[LoginCount], [c0].[MetaDescription], [c0].[MetaKeywords], [c0].[MetaTitle], [c0].[ModDate], [c0].[ModUser], [c0].[Name], [c0].[OrderNo], [c0].[OrjId], [c0].[OrjId1], [c0].[TemplateType], [c0].[VideoLink]
        FROM [ContentPage] AS [c0]
        WHERE [c0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t] ON [c].[ContentPageId] = [t].[Id]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [d].[Id], [d].[Alt], [d].[BIMFileId], [d].[BannerImageId], [d].[CadDataId], [d].[CreaDate], [d].[CreaUser], [d].[DocumentId], [d].[GalleryId], [d].[Guid], [d].[IsDeleted], [d].[IsStatus], [d].[Link], [d].[LoginCount], [d].[ModDate], [d].[ModUser], [d].[Name], [d].[OrderNo], [d].[PictureId], [d].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d].[ThumbImageId], [d].[Title], [d].[Types], [d].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d]
        WHERE [d].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[ThumbImageId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [d0].[Id], [d0].[Alt], [d0].[BIMFileId], [d0].[BannerImageId], [d0].[CadDataId], [d0].[CreaDate], [d0].[CreaUser], [d0].[DocumentId], [d0].[GalleryId], [d0].[Guid], [d0].[IsDeleted], [d0].[IsStatus], [d0].[Link], [d0].[LoginCount], [d0].[ModDate], [d0].[ModUser], [d0].[Name], [d0].[OrderNo], [d0].[PictureId], [d0].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d0].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d0].[ThumbImageId], [d0].[Title], [d0].[Types], [d0].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d0]
        WHERE [d0].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[PictureId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [d1].[Id], [d1].[Alt], [d1].[BIMFileId], [d1].[BannerImageId], [d1].[CadDataId], [d1].[CreaDate], [d1].[CreaUser], [d1].[DocumentId], [d1].[GalleryId], [d1].[Guid], [d1].[IsDeleted], [d1].[IsStatus], [d1].[Link], [d1].[LoginCount], [d1].[ModDate], [d1].[ModUser], [d1].[Name], [d1].[OrderNo], [d1].[PictureId], [d1].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d1].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d1].[ThumbImageId], [d1].[Title], [d1].[Types], [d1].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d1]
        WHERE [d1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t2] ON [c].[Id] = [t2].[BannerImageId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [f].[Id], [f].[CreaDate], [f].[CreaUser], [f].[DescName], [f].[IsDeleted], [f].[IsStatus], [f].[LoginCount], [f].[Mail], [f].[MailCC], [f].[ModDate], [f].[ModUser], [f].[Name], [f].[OrderNo]
        FROM [FormType] AS [f]
        WHERE [f].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t3] ON [c].[FormTypeId] = [t3].[Id]
    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND ((LOWER([c].[Link]) = @__ToLower_0) AND ([c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)))
) AS [t4]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[BannerButtonText], [c1].[BannerText], [c1].[ButtonLink], [c1].[ButtonText], [c1].[ContentData], [c1].[ContentOrderNo], [c1].[ContentPageId], [c1].[ContentShort], [c1].[ContentTypesId], [c1].[CreaDate], [c1].[CreaUser], [c1].[Description], [c1].[ExternalLink], [c1].[FormTypeId], [c1].[IsActive], [c1].[IsBayi], [c1].[IsBireysel], [c1].[IsClick], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[IsEndustri], [c1].[IsFooterMenu], [c1].[IsGallery], [c1].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c1].[IsHeaderMenu], [c1].[IsInteral], [c1].[IsInterax], [c1].[IsIntersecure], [c1].[IsInterwall], [c1].[IsMap], [c1].[IsMimar], [c1].[IsPublish], [c1].[IsSideMenu], [c1].[IsStatus], [c1].[LangId], [c1].[Link], [c1].[LoginCount], [c1].[MetaDescription], [c1].[MetaKeywords], [c1].[MetaTitle], [c1].[ModDate], [c1].[ModUser], [c1].[Name], [c1].[OrderNo], [c1].[OrjId], [c1].[OrjId1], [c1].[TemplateType], [c1].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [t4].[Id] = [t5].[ContentPageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BIMFileId], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CadDataId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d2].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]

    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t6] ON [t4].[Id] = [t6].[GalleryId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BIMFileId], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CadDataId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d3].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]

    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t7] ON [t4].[Id] = [t7].[DocumentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d4].[Id], [d4].[Alt], [d4].[BIMFileId], [d4].[BannerImageId], [d4].[CadDataId], [d4].[CreaDate], [d4].[CreaUser], [d4].[DocumentId], [d4].[GalleryId], [d4].[Guid], [d4].[IsDeleted], [d4].[IsStatus], [d4].[Link], [d4].[LoginCount], [d4].[ModDate], [d4].[ModUser], [d4].[Name], [d4].[OrderNo], [d4].[PictureId], [d4].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d4].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d4].[ThumbImageId], [d4].[Title], [d4].[Types], [d4].[data_class]

    FROM [Documents] AS [d5]
    WHERE [d5].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t9] ON [t4].[Id] = [t9].[TechnicalDocumentId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d6].[Id], [d6].[Alt], [d6].[BIMFileId], [d6].[BannerImageId], [d6].[CadDataId], [d6].[CreaDate], [d6].[CreaUser], [d6].[DocumentId], [d6].[GalleryId], [d6].[Guid], [d6].[IsDeleted], [d6].[IsStatus], [d6].[Link], [d6].[LoginCount], [d6].[ModDate], [d6].[ModUser], [d6].[Name], [d6].[OrderNo], [d6].[PictureId], [d6].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d6].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d6].[ThumbImageId], [d6].[Title], [d6].[Types], [d6].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d6]
    WHERE [d6].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t10] ON [t4].[Id] = [t10].[CadDataId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d7].[Id], [d7].[Alt], [d7].[BIMFileId], [d7].[BannerImageId], [d7].[CadDataId], [d7].[CreaDate], [d7].[CreaUser], [d7].[DocumentId], [d7].[GalleryId], [d7].[Guid], [d7].[IsDeleted], [d7].[IsStatus], [d7].[Link], [d7].[LoginCount], [d7].[ModDate], [d7].[ModUser], [d7].[Name], [d7].[OrderNo], [d7].[PictureId], [d7].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d7].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d7].[ThumbImageId], [d7].[Title], [d7].[Types], [d7].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d7]
    WHERE [d7].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t11] ON [t4].[Id] = [t11].[BIMFileId]
LEFT JOIN (

    ) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[PictureId]

        SELECT [d1].[Id], [d1].[Alt], [d1].[BIMFileId], [d1].[BannerImageId], [d1].[CadDataId], [d1].[CreaDate], [d1].[CreaUser], [d1].[DocumentId], [d1].[GalleryId], [d1].[Guid], [d1].[IsDeleted], [d1].[IsStatus], [d1].[Link], [d1].[LoginCount], [d1].[ModDate], [d1].[ModUser], [d1].[Name], [d1].[OrderNo], [d1].[PictureId], [d1].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d1].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d1].[ThumbImageId], [d1].[Title], [d1].[Types], [d1].[data_class]
        FROM [Documents] AS [d1]
        WHERE [d1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[BannerImageId]
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT [f].[Id], [f].[CreaDate], [f].[CreaUser], [f].[DescName], [f].[IsDeleted], [f].[IsStatus], [f].[LoginCount], [f].[Mail], [f].[MailCC], [f].[ModDate], [f].[ModUser], [f].[Name], [f].[OrderNo]
        FROM [FormType] AS [f]
        WHERE [f].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
    ) AS [t2] ON [c].[FormTypeId] = [t2].[Id]
    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND ((([c].[IsActive] = CAST(1 AS bit)) AND ([c].[IsPublish] = CAST(1 AS bit))) AND (LOWER([c].[Link]) = @__ToLower_0))
) AS [t3]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BIMFileId], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CadDataId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d2].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d2]
    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [t3].[Id] = [t4].[GalleryId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BIMFileId], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CadDataId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d3].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d3]
    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [t3].[Id] = [t5].[DocumentId]
ORDER BY [t3].[Id], [t3].[Id0], [t3].[Id1], [t3].[Id2], [t3].[Id3], [t4].[Id], [t5].[Id]"
